        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18464317-night-owl">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review">arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=angsty-romance">angsty-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=hot-n-steamy-romance">hot-n-steamy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer738630480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4911386819299515961">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>5++++ <b> “Mm.” “little bird” “Mr. Frostypants” </b> Kisses<br/><br/>So...the synopsis hooked me. This is a pretty original concept, at least as far as I was concerned and it definitely piqued my interest. When it comes to reading erotica…I have one expectation - <b>insanely</b> hot sex…everything else just makes me a happier camper. Well, this book achieved that...and then some. I never knew what to expect with the story line or characters and up to the epilogue, I loved every dire</span>
  <span id="freeText4911386819299515961" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>5++++ <b> “Mm.” “little bird” “Mr. Frostypants” </b> Kisses<br><br>So...the synopsis hooked me. This is a pretty original concept, at least as far as I was concerned and it definitely piqued my interest. When it comes to reading erotica…I have one expectation - <b>insanely</b> hot sex…everything else just makes me a happier camper. Well, this book achieved that...and then some. I never knew what to expect with the story line or characters and up to the epilogue, I loved every direction it took me.<br><br>Matthew Robert Sky Jr....M. Pierce…<i>Mr. Frostypants</i>...Matt Matt Matt...what am I going to do with you. He's like the ‘anti hero’. He's snarky and brooding and not in the normal sexy way I usually love...in a different sexy way that I still love equally as much. He’s surly and sour, he's secretive and just...an enigma…but that’s what made me like him more. What else did I like about Matt…I like that he made list’s…I liked that he had an unconventional pet (I’ll get to that in a little bit)...I liked the necklace that he got Hannah *<i>sigh</i>*...and I even liked his personality, as strange as that may sound. He’s so interesting and different from the normal BBF’s. It was an interesting dilemma because I never disliked Matt completely but he doesn't make it easy to just fall in love with him....until you see him completely with Hannah. Then all bets are off. Plus it helps that he’s hot…don’t judge me, I am a little superficial.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425933ra/850441.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘I had never felt such longing in my life. My whole body responded to the idea of Hannah near me.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Hannah Catalano…little bird...oh, I straight up loved Hannah from the get go. She's so likeable, genuine, real...funny, authentic...I just liked her! I liked her relationship with Matt...her tenacity, her attitude...the way she approached things...especially where Matt was concerned. She knew delving into a relationship with him wasn’t going to be easy…but I <i>know</i> she wasn’t expecting what happened. I’ll give her this much, the girl has got some balls...she's not a push over and she's not weak...she is slightly different when it comes to Matt and his charms but...come on now, that can be forgiven. What girl isn’t a little googly-eyed and out of character when it comes to the man who can knock us on our ass.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414979202i/11713299._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘Was I asking for trouble?<br>Tonight, trouble was a beautiful body standing next to a beautiful car right outside my house, waiting for me.<br>I didn’t feel a single twinge of fear.<br>I felt raw elation.’ </b> </blockquote><br>So Matt and Hannah do not have the typical meeting. By far. And I <b>liked</b> that! It's not out of the realm of possibility...while some of it may have been a bit…kinky, it worked for me. You cannot really call what develops with Matt and Hannah ‘insta-love’ because they have interacted for months - granted on a purely professional, strictly business level - but...they are not strangers by far. That being said, things do progress rather quickly once that line has been crossed...and there is no turning back. Another thing I loved. :-) I guess that is another thing I loved about Matt, once he figured out his feelings, he was sold…there may have been ‘extenuating circumstances’ that made things more difficult, but the way he felt about Hannah was concrete.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382331668ra/5825139.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘“Beautiful man. I wish you could see yourself. You look lost.”<br>“I feel lost,” I whispered.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Hannah and Matt are <b>hooooot</b>! Scorching…sizzling…blazing…ten alarm fire…that kind of <b>HOT</b> - am I painting a clear picture? Like all out <i>smoking</i>, it is hands down some of the best sex I have <b>ever</b> read. I say this with no shame…I was panting during some of the scenes. Matt is dominant and demanding and all kinds of yumminess. Now, don’t get me wrong - the sex is not the only thing about them that this dirty book whore loved. Watching Matts personality open up more and change now that he is experiencing Hannah first hand…he morphed into this super insanely loveable Matt - the core essence of him was still there, still surely and sour, but he was loving, sweet and receptive to Hannah. He treated her with such care and yet still managed to fuck her on a desk and out in the wilderness...sounds pretty perfect right? Yup…it was.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382331668ra/5825140.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘…I was wrapped around her finger. She gazed over her shoulder with half-lidded eyes and whispered my name. Why did I think I had any power over Hannah? I was hers.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Alright, well there is more to this story than meets the eye...I don't do spoilers...but like I said I didn't see most of what was coming. You know what else I didn't see coming...Lawrence. Matts pet rabbit. Yeah...pretty much the one of the most awesome things I have ever read in a book. And once again...it makes me love Matt more. Just sayin. I also loved Chrissy, Hannah's sister - because she made me laugh. I love Nate, Matts brother, because he's the best big bro in the world. I loved the plot because it was very unpredictable and I never knew what was going to happen and while, yes it is an erotica, there was a significant amount of angst IMO.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382331668ra/5825141.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘”My body…craves your body.” Matt bounced me again and we moaned together. “It f-feels the distance…when we’re apart. Hannah, I can’t be apart from you.”<br>“You never have to be,” I said.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Another thing I loved...the writing. It's crisp and clean while being descriptive and precise. It's a very unique style and it just flowed throughout the entire book for me. The dialogue is fantastic, Matt and Hannah's inner thoughts are perfection and there is so much sarcasm and whit weaved into the book, I couldn’t get enough. Also, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7258437.M__Pierce" title="M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">M. Pierce</a> is a very intellectual writer - there are words in this book that I have never seen used in a romance. That's <i>awesome</i>! We switch back and forth, alternating chapters from Hannah and Matts POV's and both were written <b>extremely</b> well. Once you realize the pattern it's relatively easy to keep up with and I enjoyed having both of their POV’s - there was never any backtracking or redundancy, the characters might address their feelings in regards to something that previously happened but we never had to go thru the event all over again from their POV. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382331668ra/5825142.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘The hollowness inside of me didn’t shrink. It expanded until it seemed to press at the limits of my being. I became less than a shell of myself. I was a fine limning – a suggestion of Hannah Catalano.<br>One day, I thought, I wouldn’t even be that.<br>I understood how people fall apart.<br>I understood how dangerous it is to let someone become your whole life, and how powerless we are to prevent it. <i>Never deny me</i>, Matt once said. As if I had a choice.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Okay so now I must address the ending. The last chapter is fabulous. <b>Perfection</b>. Great ending for Hannah and Matt, even though it's not as conclusive and concrete as I usually like. But…then there is the epilogue. If you don't like cliffs - do not read the epilogue, problem solved! With the way <i>Night Owl</i> ends, it could have been a standalone…but it’s not a standalone. It’s the first book in a trilogy…so of course there needs to be a <i>reason</i> for you to read the next book...the epilogue is that reason. I have so many questions and I am not a very happy girl about the cliff - and an epilogue of two pages did that to me! The 'great and horrible' epilogue aside…I really loved this book. Everything about it worked for me and I couldn't get enough. And even though the epilogue cliff’d me, I <b>can't wait</b> for the next book…so it worked! If <i>Night Owl</i> is any indication of what is to be expected for the rest of the series, count me in. This book is astoundingly well written, practically flawless in my opinion and if you're a lover of contemporary romance, erotica and indie books, this is by far one of the best choices out there.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382331668i/5825143._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4911386819299515961" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer9257132016974736571"><b>Night Owl/Matt</b> and <b>Little Bird/Hannah</b> met online and are writing a collaborative story. To keep this relationship strictly anonymous Matt has rules: <blockquote>
  <b>"No specifics, no last name, no phone number. Nothing. I don't want to know you, and I don't want you to know me. We write together online, that's it. I'm not looking for a new friend. I'm looking for a writing partner."</b>
</blockquote><br/>Matt's plan works until Hannah starts bucking the system. Little accidental e-mails from Hannah's personal account leads to Mat</span>
  <span id="freeText9257132016974736571" style="display:none"><b>Night Owl/Matt</b> and <b>Little Bird/Hannah</b> met online and are writing a collaborative story. To keep this relationship strictly anonymous Matt has rules: <blockquote>
  <b>"No specifics, no last name, no phone number. Nothing. I don't want to know you, and I don't want you to know me. We write together online, that's it. I'm not looking for a new friend. I'm looking for a writing partner."</b>
</blockquote><br>Matt's plan works until Hannah starts bucking the system. Little accidental e-mails from Hannah's personal account leads to Matt wanting to know more about his writing partner. Their attraction starts out cerebral but turns physical. <br><br>I love the way they met and their conversations through Skype. A perfect book for November because November is NaNoWriMo <a href="http://nanowrimo.org/" rel="nofollow noopener">(National Novel Writing Month).</a> Several authors got their start from NaNoWriMo. <br><br>Very interesting that the author of<u> Night Owl </u> is Matt's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[pen name. I noticed that the first time we learned Matt's pen name. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Does this book have cheating in it?</b> I'm not a fan of cheating. I avoid books with this subject matter because I don't find them enjoyable. Now, back to the question...I'm going to answer in a spoiler in case someone doesn't want to know. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Let's start by defining what the word means-&gt; <b>Cheating</b> is when one person has a significant other and performs any type of intimate acts with another person. <br><br>Matt has a girl friend but she's not in the picture because she's traveling. How the author writes the story it doesn't bother me that Matt has gf and maybe that's because she's away on a trip with her parents. Matt's feelings towards his gf aren't those of being in love but more of companionship.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18681804.Night_Owl__The_Night_Owl_Trilogy___1_" title="Night Owl (The Night Owl Trilogy, #1) by M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1381909348s/18681804.jpg" alt="Night Owl (The Night Owl Trilogy, #1) by M. Pierce" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18744040.Last_Light__The_Night_Owl_Trilogy___2_" title="Last Light (The Night Owl Trilogy, #2) by M. Pierce" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png" alt="Last Light (The Night Owl Trilogy, #2) by M. Pierce" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>3 books in the series. <br>No cliffhanger <b> unless</b> you read the <i>epilogue.</i> <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_challenges/549008" rel="nofollow noopener">180th book of 2013</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer758023595" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10799716643149526389"><b>4.5 Stars<br/>Sometimes you read a book that takes you a little out of your comfort zone. I was open to this due to the terrific review by my pal DKristin... and thought I would go for it.<br/><br/>Although I could see from the start I was captivated by the feel, writing and set up, it quickly moved to an area that made me take a moment. I need to adjust my mindset to the verbiage used during the sex between the characters. Once I was clear on the participation and desire of both on this, I was good to go with</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10799716643149526389" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars<br>Sometimes you read a book that takes you a little out of your comfort zone. I was open to this due to the terrific review by my pal DKristin... and thought I would go for it.<br><br>Although I could see from the start I was captivated by the feel, writing and set up, it quickly moved to an area that made me take a moment. I need to adjust my mindset to the verbiage used during the sex between the characters. Once I was clear on the participation and desire of both on this, I was good to go with the rest of the story. <br><br>This was something very unusual... a love story which had a pull and life of its own. </b>Neither seemed able to fight it and in the end... both were tied to each other without any beginning or end... they just were.<br><br>Read the blur... it tells the story... and I actually think you are best off not knowing too much... you will appreciate it more. <br><br>This is part of a trilogy but you are not left with a major cliffy... just a hint of something that is coming down the line. I will be right in line for the next chapter... this is that good.<br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

All this excitment and swooning totally clouded my judgement. I knew I'd be having hard time with Night Owl and yet I was stupid enough to actually 'read' this *facepalm*. I think my brain had an accident and turned off for awhile. There is so no other explanation, why I would torture myself. I wish I could forgot picking it up. I kn</span>
  <span id="freeText15715328985135003211" style="display:none"><br><b> DNF-ed at 45% </b><br><br><i>I know there is supposed to be no rating, but I couldn't stop myslef </i><br><br><br><br>I don't know how it even happened that I finally gave in and started reading it. All this excitment and swooning totally clouded my judgement. I knew I'd be having hard time with Night Owl and yet I was stupid enough to actually 'read' this *facepalm*. I think my brain had an accident and turned off for awhile. There is so no other explanation, why I would torture myself. I wish I could forgot picking it up. I know, I know... If the wishes were horses, begars would ride... and so on. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384363292ra/6858254.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i> Contains spoilers </i>
</b><br><br><br>What didn't work out for me?<br><br><b>1. CHEATING, LYING BASTARDS ARE NOT DROOL WORTHY HEROES. <b> THEY ARE NOT!!!!!! </b> *takes a deep breath * </b><br><br>I can't believe Matt started cheating on his girlfriend of two years, because he found a chick on the internet that made his dick hard. What a fucking asshole! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298611ra/685957.gif" width="400/&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I just have &lt;u&gt;zero&lt;/u&gt; tolerance policy over something like this. I can't handle it. Nope. This is a totall deal breaker. Even after Matt had a phone sex with Hannah and cheated on Bethany this way, I was able to calm down and rationalize that he can still break up with Beth and then I have a clean start with Hannah. Well, he didn't do that. Actually he started having lots of lots of sex with Hannah and she didn't even know about his girlfriend. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img src=" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2. THERE IS LITERALLY NO PLOT. JUST SEX. <br><br>They meet on the internet, write, jerk off together, have phone sex and start having 'real' sex.<br>There is no feelings - no love, no caring, nothing. Only lust, FOR A FREAKING PERSON THEY DIDN'T MEET!!!!!!!!! They have sex, and more sex... you get the jazz, mind you I've read only 45%.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381656597ra/5150914.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3. SEX. <br><br>Well having sex without kissing someone before is... totall turn-off. Kisses are, in my opinion sexier and more important than the 'insert penis into vagina' thing. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> "Despite last night and the best sex of my life, Hannah and I hadn't truly kissed yet." </blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432888ra/870743.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Still, I tried. I really did. But even Matt's dirty talking (and I'm a slut for some smutty talk) wasn't enough to make me read longer. After the scene in the strip club I was done. <b> Shoul've done it earlier, though. </b> I don't even want to know how it ended, but if I had to guess, it probably went like this <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Hannah found out about Beth and him being Matt Pierce, Beth found out about Hannah and Matt realized he loves Hannah. So there would be totall mindfuck with cliffhanger or make up sex.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>The best thing? Laurence the bunny. I have a rabbit (a pet, get your mind of the gutter!) myself and love, loove him. <br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13739741671906848113"><b>5 Mm…ing stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383523435i/6586358.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Matt & Hannah’s <s>relationship</s> arrangement begins as a simple agreement. Two writers co-authoring a story. But Matt has rules. No specifics, no last names, no phone numbers, no pictures… But even when these two stay within the rules the lines start to blur. <br/><br/>But when a mistake is made, it’s too late for Matt to clear his mind of what he now knows. One woman is driving his fantasies and this one woman is now within reach. But Matt’s life is not a simple one. Desperate for his privacy </span>
  <span id="freeText13739741671906848113" style="display:none"><b>5 Mm…ing stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383523435i/6586358.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Matt &amp; Hannah’s <s>relationship</s> arrangement begins as a simple agreement. Two writers co-authoring a story. But Matt has rules. No specifics, no last names, no phone numbers, no pictures… But even when these two stay within the rules the lines start to blur. <br><br>But when a mistake is made, it’s too late for Matt to clear his mind of what he now knows. One woman is driving his fantasies and this one woman is now within reach. But Matt’s life is not a simple one. Desperate for his privacy and a heartbreaking past that was both in and out of his control; Matt begins a dangerous game with Hannah, his little bird.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383523435i/6586359.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Erotic and haunting. I clung to my Kindle the entire time. This story grabbed you completely from the start. Flirty messages that started off simple and innocent, suddenly turning into scorching moments of unraveling self-control and let’s not forget his dirty mouth. <br><br>Matt played both the hero and the anti-hero, concealing his identity and his relationship from Hannah. <br><br><blockquote><i><b>”Don’t give me that look. I’m trying to teach you this mysterious skill, one that you seem to lack. It’s called how to say goodbye.”<br>I smiled and rubbed the back of my neck.<br>“What are you grinning at?” she said.<br>“I never want to.” I said<br>“What? Never want to what?”<br>“I never want to learn how to say goodbye.”</b></i></blockquote>
<br><br>And although I typically wince when it comes to any type of infidelity in a book, there was just something about this situation that was different. Less troubling, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Bethany did not exist as anything more than a few keystrokes within the story, her presence was non-existent when Hannah &amp; Matt were together. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383523435i/6586360.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This felt like two stories perfectly woven together. There was the fantastic smutty parts that had you panting and squirming and then there was the hauntingly painful moments that had holding your breath. <br><br><blockquote><i><b>”He dressed like sex, drove the sexiest car I’d ever been in, and bought me the Cadillac of sex toys without blinking.”</b></i></blockquote>
<br><br>Together these two parts formed a brilliant story that even with all the rave reviews, was still unexpected. There was beauty and pure lust in the writing.<br><br><blockquote><i><b>”The best days are the first to flee.”<br><br>“The tiny endless peeping of the chicks was breaking my fucking heart. I would probably cry when I got into the barn. That’s what I usually did. Finally, I captured one of the chicks. I cupped its body to my chest. Little bird, I thought. Soft warm little bird.”</b></i></blockquote>
<br><br><b>Matt broke down Hannah systematically and put her back together with each pounding thrust. </b> Although we did not get too much back-story with Hannah, beyond simple things she shared, we got to know Matt deeply. We saw both pleasure and pain; told both from Hannah’s point of view and his own.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383523435i/6586361._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I am not sure what to exactly expect with the second installment of this trilogy, the epilogue leaves us with quite a few questions, but for some reason it did not leave me fearful of what was to come. <br>I absolutely fell in love with this book. Every scene, every word… </i><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Being curious, I grabbed my kindle, loaded it up and – BAM! The intensity of this story lured me in like the proverbial fish on a hook. I was savagely devouring each word. I LOVED it and could not tear myself away. It took me a while to mull this one over and formulate cohesive thoughts, because this story evoked so man</span>
  <span id="freeText16957361397511244665" style="display:none">4.5 Nocturnally Sinful Stars <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sizzlingpages.com">http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspot.com">http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384400458i/6867890._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I decided to check out “NIGHT OWL”, the latest book everyone’s talking about. Being curious, I grabbed my kindle, loaded it up and – BAM! The intensity of this story lured me in like the proverbial fish on a hook. I was savagely devouring each word. I LOVED it and could not tear myself away. It took me a while to mull this one over and formulate cohesive thoughts, because this story evoked so many emotions for me.<br> <br>Matt Sky, a best selling author writing under the alias M. Pierce (hmm), meets Hannah Catalano on-line while collaborating on a story. He is a sexy, temperamental and mysterious man. Hannah, also a writer, is a beautiful, sweet, fun loving girl. While working together, Matt puts in place several stipulations on their “relationship”. No sharing personal information and under no circumstances will he reveal the fact he is the M. Pierce. All is well and they are focused on their work until Matt stumbles across a photo of Hannah. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384429430i/6874881._SX540_.jpg" width='“600"' height='“800"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><i>
  <b><br>Sad things seem truest to me</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384401004i/6868086.jpg" width='“600"' height='“800"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b><br><br>"You are always deceiving me," she whispered..."Always, Matt, always speaking to me from any mouth but your own. Don't you know that I love you? I see you under all your lies, and I always find you.”</b>
</i><br><br>The more Matt interacts with Hannah, the more things get personal. Matt becomes obsessed and desperately needs to connect with Hannah - learn everything about her. Eventually, his boundaries are crossed and their telephone conversations turn into sizzling phone sex scenes. But, their relationship is forbidden and Matt’s constant need to hear her voice, is tearing him apart. Trying to remain emotionally detached from Hannah becomes taxing. All bets are off when she moves back home to Colorado, right in his back yard. As destiny plays its hand, these two finally meet. And then, all hell breaks loose.<br><br>This book contained extremely hot, extremely erotic scenes. Matt and Hannah get-it-on, and fast. From scandalous public displays affection to blindfolding, ball-gagging spank fests, this couple is HOT and extraordinarily kinky. Rawr…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384429841i/6874941.jpg" width="400" height='“400"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>“You’re my slut...”<br>"You don’t give me pleasure, do you understand? I take take it from you.”<br>“Hannah, God. Do you want this? Feel what you’re doing to me."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384430084i/6874994.jpg" width="400" height='“400"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>'Best sex of my life: bent over a desk and belted'</b>
</i><b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384400162i/6867773.jpg" width="400" height='“400"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>'...a hole in his life that should not be filled. It was over, and it could not be over because he could not forget. She would become all that emptiness. In that, there was a comfort.<br>Nothing lasts forever, and nothing ever ends.’</b><br><br><br>Aside from the sexually provocative story line, there is a lot more going on. This story is multifaceted. Matt was one of the most interesting literary characters I have ever come across. When we first meet Matt, he was a rude, cocky bastard. His mysterious and dominant ways allures Hannah like a moth to a flame. But, as his arrogance fades, it is clear that Matt cares deeply for her. His dominant characteristics barely scrape the surface of his persona. He is vulnerable, neurotic and has deep emotional issues. His soul bares so many secrets and he has difficulties dealing with the guilt for starting their relationship.<br><br>Matt is very sensitive (No, the crying after the shagging did not bother me. Real men cry…. Gideon Cross and Christian Grey’s shed tears did not diminish their alpha-male personalities - neither does Matt’s). He’s extremely introverted, paranoid and secretive. Matt craves anonymity and control. He cannot cope without these mechanisms in place. If exposed, he will fall apart… and he does. It was gut wrenching witnessing Matt lose everything and his world shatter. He becomes a prisoner in his own mind, a recluse. Decimated and alone, Matt turns back to old habits and his life is in turmoil.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384400162i/6867775._SY540_.jpg" width='“300"' height='“400"' alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"I think I've always loved you," I whispered. "I felt something since we met, since we first started writing together. It was like I had loved you without knowing you, and the love was in me, waiting to happen. So you can’t apologize, Matt. It's you I love. There's no why about it."</b>
</i><br><br>Hannah is Matt’s "little bird". When Matt’s world spirals off it’s axis, it is Hannah who heals him. She loves Matt fiercely, and it is that love that gives her the strength to forgive. Despite the obstacles that lie in their path, Hannah over comes the hurdles and takes Matt under her wing. Her will is strong and she has the ability to piece their lives back together. <br><br>With out revealing any of the plot, I will say that, for me, there is a fair amount of symbolism in this story: <br><br>The Rabbit:<br><br>Matt’s pet, Laurence, is a lovable bunny. To me, Laurence is also extension of his character. Like the rabbit, Matt is timid, fearful and reserved. <br><br>The Manatee:<br>While Matt is ill, Hannah gives him a stuff animal manatee. A rather odd gift to give and Matt develops a strange attachment to it. He goes nowhere without this talisman. Manatees are gentle, loving, trustworthy and peaceful creatures. Much like the presence of Hannah in his life.<br><br><br>Oh the epilogue…. there’s another conundrum. Can’t say much about it with out spoiling the twist ending. You’ll have to read it to believe it or… not. I, however, have several theories formulated about it’s meaning and what’s to come… I highly recommend reading this sensual, mysterious tale and join me in the long wait to see what the future holds for Matt and Hannah.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381602476ra/5085946.gif" width="400" height='“500"' alt="description”/&gt;" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/753793613?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss" href="/user/show/6423103-miss">Miss</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18681804-night-owl">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=waste-of-time">waste-of-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=whattings">whattings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=money-whores">money-whores</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=no">no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=asshole-hero">asshole-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=tstl-heroine">tstl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=the-burning-bed">the-burning-bed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=sock-puppets">sock-puppets</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6423103-miss?shelf=when-hell-freezes-over">when-hell-freezes-over</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer753793613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15714778040162860128">****This review will undoubtedly contain spoilers :)Read at your own risk.****<br/><br/><br/><br/> The first impression that I got from the hero who stars in this story was that he was a complete asshole. His character was all over the place and I had no clue where the author was going with him. At first. Then comes the hero's first sexual interaction with the heroine and it became clear where this author was going. Yes, he/she is going there. <br/><br/> The book is lacking character development. I don't mind D/s BDSM romanc</span>
  <span id="freeText15714778040162860128" style="display:none">****This review will undoubtedly contain spoilers :)Read at your own risk.****<br><br><br><br> The first impression that I got from the hero who stars in this story was that he was a complete asshole. His character was all over the place and I had no clue where the author was going with him. At first. Then comes the hero's first sexual interaction with the heroine and it became clear where this author was going. Yes, he/she is going there. <br><br> The book is lacking character development. I don't mind D/s BDSM romance or erotica, I've read tons of it. There's no set up for that type of relationship between the hero and heroine in this book. Lines are not drawn, and no boundaries set, it's just suddenly there and the reader is supposed to believe it.<br><br> Break out the book "D/s BDSM books for Dummies". Let's take the Safe, Sane, and Consensual out of the equation people. Let's continue with trope after trope, and sprinkle with clichés. Rich, broody hero, who is both hot, and demanding. Check. Down on her luck heroine who has an insatiable sexual appetite. Check. Not long into the book I had begun to question the hero's sanity because he was a little off in my opinion. He enjoyed humiliating the heroine by calling her names such as greedy slut. She enjoys being debased, so who am I to judge? The reason it bothered me was because the hero often questions himself as to why he enjoys humiliating her the way he does. <br><br> "That's nice baby, I like that noise. I like those embarrassing noises. You yowl like a cat when I fuck you hard, and you whine and beg like a dog. This might be my favorite, though. You're grunting like a pig. Does that mean you like this?" I shoved my finger in another centimeter. Hannah shuddered. "Where's my noise? Come on baby, start grunting. If you don't make this good for me I won't fuck you."<br><br>LET ME OUT OF HERE!<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383685194ra/6632711.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"<br><br> Collar, nipple clamps, gag, and domestic discipline are quickly introduced with no prior warning or lead up. I was thinking that this was a first for this H, and since I had already begun to question his sanity, I quickly began to question the heroines safety as well. We do later find out that he has participated in these kind of activities with previous partner's before, but not to what extent. Meanwhile, God/god is mentioned so often in this book that I was certain he was going to appear as a character in the book. Normally this is not something I notice, but it was there over 200 times.<br><br> Through all of this the hero has been keeping secrets from the heroine. First he has a live in girlfriend that he failed to mention, and he has also been hiding the fact that he is a best selling author. Her favorite author. He has lied and schemed to keep these secrets from her. Now that he is falling in love, the guilt begins to tear him apart. This is when we finally get some depth in the story.<br><br> Every thing comes down on this hero at once. He finally does the right thing and breaks up with the girlfriend, but she gets even by outing him to the world as best selling author M. Pierce. No longer safe with his anonymity the heroine finds out about the girlfriend, and who he is. She leaves him. He falls apart. His devastation was absolute and heartbreaking to read. I didn't care for him during the first half of the book due to what's mentioned above, but now my heart hurt reading his breakdown. The rest of the book is spent with the heroine dealing with his mental health and trying to salvage their relationship. There is a sex scene just before the end that disturbed the hell out of me, pretty much ruining the second half of the book. The hero is still mentally unstable at this time when he subjects the heroine to a beating from his belt out of the blue. At the beginning of the whipping he's being pretty manic and she is scared. He goes on to tell her that she is soaking wet and loving the pain and she admits to liking it. By then it was just too much and too brutal.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383694443ra/6635789.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> The book ends with a HFN, but I still have no idea why he is the way that he is. No diagnosis was given about his mental health and none of the questions I had were answered in the end.<br><br> Then we have the Epilogue....... <br><br> A certain scene from a movie crossed my mind after reading that epilogue. You may know which one I'm referring to but just in case.... Ace Ventura: Pet Detective<br><br>Lois Einhorn is Ray Finkle, Ray Finkle is Lois Einhorn! <br><br> <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15714778040162860128" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/756934214" />
    <a title="readtoomuch" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9128827-readtoomuch"><img alt="readtoomuch" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1385146497p2/9128827.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/756934214?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="readtoomuch" class="user" itemprop="url" name="readtoomuch" href="/user/show/9128827-readtoomuch">readtoomuch</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18681804-night-owl">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9128827-readtoomuch?shelf=ackorgiddyway-itchesorgiddybay">ackorgiddyway-itchesorgiddybay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9128827-readtoomuch?shelf=would-not-recommend">would-not-recommend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9128827-readtoomuch?shelf=dungeon">dungeon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756934214" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13769892536754813197">1/2 star rating<br/><br/>What was this? Seriously, what the hell kind of story was this?<br/><br/>I read a lot. I read books in many different genres, including many in the Erotica genre, and what I label as the dark/twisted sub-genres and the BDSM sub-genres. This book is a horrid not-funny joke to those genres, as is the belief that this author's writing could be labeled as "good" or "well written." No. This "book" was not well written, because if it was there would have been <i>character development</i> and <i>plot develo</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13769892536754813197" style="display:none">1/2 star rating<br /><br />What was this? Seriously, what the hell kind of story was this?<br /><br />I read a lot. I read books in many different genres, including many in the Erotica genre, and what I label as the dark/twisted sub-genres and the BDSM sub-genres. This book is a horrid not-funny joke to those genres, as is the belief that this author's writing could be labeled as "good" or "well written." No. This "book" was not well written, because if it was there would have been <i>character development</i> and <i>plot development</i>. There was little to none of both. I don't care that this is part of a trilogy, because a foundation for a worthy story to read was not there. <br /><br />There was not sufficient enough information or characterization of either of the main characters to really understand why they are the way they are, and why they act the way they do. There was nothing to make me understand the main character's actions enough to be empathetic. Were hints of the main character's mental instability and possible bipolar disorder supposed to make me sympathetic enough to lessen the harshness of the humiliation and the abusively handled BDSM practices he puts Hannah through? Are you kidding me?<br /><br />I felt nothing but disgust for the characters, and ultimately, the author of Night Owl. There is an <b>uneducated and demeaning type of BDSM relationship between the two main characters</b> that made me cringe in horror and disgust. Throughout this story, the author clearly revealed a lack of knowledge and research about the practices and dynamics of BDSM, and the relationship that should be developed in this lifestyle. Instead, the inept use of BDSM is used as (what I read as) abuse and debasement towards a woman who does not know any better, and a main character who humiliates as an outlet for ????. This is not funny, and I find it appalling. <br /><br />I am rarely on GR. I don't usually write reviews, because I would rather spend those few minutes reading. I don't usually read reviews, because I like to make my own judgement about a book without any preconceived hype or negativity. However, a good friend encouraged me to express my opinion since I felt so strongly about this book. I will <u>never</u> read anything by this author again. I would <u>not</u> recommend this book to anyone. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13769892536754813197" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_755028776" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755028776" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755028776?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18681804-night-owl">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755028776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4689993018591850288"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br/><br/>∞ Matt, aka Night Owl, and Hannah, aka Little Bird, meet through an online writing site and become writing partners. There's suppose to be absolutely no personal information exchanged but Hannah accidentally crosses the line and that sets things in motion.<br/><br/>∞ One of the problems is that Matt has a lot of secrets and slowly we find out he's had some problems in his past that are not pretty. It's almost like there are two sides to him. The situation with Hannah takes him by surprise </span>
  <span id="freeText4689993018591850288" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>∞ Matt, aka Night Owl, and Hannah, aka Little Bird, meet through an online writing site and become writing partners. There's suppose to be absolutely no personal information exchanged but Hannah accidentally crosses the line and that sets things in motion.<br><br>∞ One of the problems is that Matt has a lot of secrets and slowly we find out he's had some problems in his past that are not pretty. It's almost like there are two sides to him. The situation with Hannah takes him by surprise and he can't keep away. <br><br>∞ Hannah doesn't help things...right from the get-go she steps right off the edge with Matt without even knowing anything about him including what he looks like. And then she gives him her address, which he scolds her for doing, but he shows up at her house anyway and after a little interlude, she takes off in the car with him. <br><br>∞ All the writing scenes were really good. I loved how they each influenced the chapters they wrote and how they like certain author quotes. <i>The Surrogate</i> sounds really good...I want to read that! <br><br>∞ Wow...Matt is a dirty talker (although I could've done without the slut comments) and him and Hannah have some hot scenes that segue into the BDSM realm.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380297835ra/682353.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>∞ Matt decides to come clean and that's when things fall apart. The hints we read about Matt come full force and it's pretty heartbreaking. I was disappointed in Hannah that she didn't try to get some answers.<br><br>∞ Thank goodness Matt has a wonderful big brother and even if he can be a bit intimidating, he does have Matt's best interests in heart. <br><br>∞ And thank goodness for the dual POVs.<br><br>∞ One of my favorite things is that Matt has a pet bunny named Laurence...I love that! The scene outside Lot 49 was a little bizarre though!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384313626i/6846630.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>∞ I did get a kick out of Matt's <i>need</i> to make lists especially since I'm a fellow list maker. Luckily, not to his extreme!<br><br>∞ I'm still not sure what caused Hannah to "wake up" but I was happy she was there for him. The manatee was really sweet. But the line that killed me was...<br><br><b>"God, I was lucky.<br><br>And fuck, I was unhappy."</b><br><br>...what in the heck does that mean?? <br><br>∞ Can we talk about the ending, aka Epilogue?? Holy cow...what in the heck was that? That was effed up...I really cannot believe the author did that. Thank goodness the next book, <i>Last Light</i> (title for now), is possibly coming out in January! (BTW...do I believe that? No way in hell! I think there's a lot more to <i>The Surrogate</i> than just a story!) <br><br>∞ <b>Footnote:</b> From doing a little reading, people are saying the author is going into the paranormal genre with the second book. Wow...maybe <i>there</i> is more to <i>The Surrogate</i>. And if you think that way and go back over things in the book, this book suddenly becomes a real head trip!<br><br>∞ <b>ETA</b> - I'm 2/2 with the male authors now. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798567i/642517.jpg" width="400" height="070" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>❈ "But there's no such thing as loneliness. There is only the idea of loneliness."<br><br>❈ "Always, Matt, always speaking to me from any mouth but your own. Don't you know that I love you? I see you under all your lies, and I always find you."<br><br>❈ "Matt... I don't want a perfect gentleman." <br><br>"What do you want?" <br><br>"You." <br><br>For the first time in months, I watched Matt's gorgeous face light up with real laughter. It was soft, enervated laughter, but it was laughter. I wanted to cry. <br><br>"Not a gentleman," he chuckled, his eyes slipping closed. <br><br>"Definitely not a gentleman," I murmured.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QtAlO20fvHDaj5vuUYehOVVcoQrCTmqsHAa1Ncf0/wY/1JTwUo7Ik2fHE2hiGVd61jfvG1mieY+6wmKDzAy4Nw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gtS5j6CEluA9U7EjCkoqfbfmr+fwrjUKqpCA+9cbg1L/0AhEnxXiA4AbOaU51Nw+NI3h9mtCJikMVFdN3OPEYw==')})
  }
